DROP TABLE Supplier;
DROP TABLE Discount;
DROP TABLE Staff;
DROP TABLE Refund;
DROP TABLE Payment;
DROP TABLE Delivery;
DROP TABLE Customer;

SET PAGESIZE 260 
ALTER SESSION SET NLS_DATE_FORMAT = "DD-MM-YYYY";

CREATE TABLE Customer(
CustomerID 	 	VARCHAR2(10) 	NOT NULL,
CustomerName 	VARCHAR2(20)	NOT NULL,
CustomerPwd		VARCHAR2(18)	CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(CustomerPwd,'^[a-zA-Z0-9@#$%^&+=_!-]{8,20}$')),
CustomerEmail 	VARCHAR2(30) 	CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(CustomerEmail,'^[a-zA-Z]\w+@(\S+)$')),
CustomerPhoneNo 	VARCHAR2(15) 	CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(CustomerPhoneNo,'^0[0-9]{2}-[0-9]{7}$')),
CustomerAddress 	VARCHAR2(30) 	NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY(CustomerID)
);

--200
CREATE TABLE Delivery(
DeliveryID			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
DeliveryStatus		VARCHAR2(15)	NOT NULL,
DeliveryCharge 		NUMBER(4,2),
DepartureDate		DATE,
ArrivedDate			DATE,
PRIMARY KEY(DeliveryID)
);

--200
CREATE TABLE Payment(
PaymentID			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
GrandTotal			NUMBER(9,2),
PaymentMethod		VARCHAR2(20)	DEFAULT 'ONLINE BANKING',
PaymentDate			DATE			,
PRIMARY KEY(PaymentID)
);

--20
CREATE TABLE Refund(
RefundID		VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
RefundDate		DATE			NOT NULL, 
RefundAmount	NUMBER(5,2) 	NOT NULL, 
RefundReason	VARCHAR2(40)	NOT NULL,
RefundStatus 	VARCHAR2(15)	NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY(RefundID) 	
);

--20
CREATE TABLE Staff(
StaffID 		VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
StaffName		VARCHAR2(25)	NOT NULL,
StaffGender 	CHAR			CHECK (StaffGender IN('M','F')),
StaffPhoneNO	VARCHAR2(15)	CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(StaffPhoneNo,'^0[0-9]{2}-[0-9]{7}$')),
StaffAddress 	VARCHAR2(37)	NOT NULL,
StaffEmail		VARCHAR2(35)	CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(StaffEmail,'^[a-zA-Z]\w+@(\S+)$')),
PRIMARY KEY(StaffID)
);

--20
CREATE TABLE Discount(
DiscountID 			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
DiscountName		VARCHAR2(25)	NOT NULL,
DiscountStatus 		VARCHAR2(15)	NOT NULL,
MinimumSpent		NUMBER(5,2)		DEFAULT 40,
DiscountPercentage	NUMBER(3,2)		NOT NULL,
MaximumCap 			NUMBER(4,2)		DEFAULT 10,
PRIMARY KEY(DiscountID)
);

--20
CREATE TABLE Supplier(
SupplierID 			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
SupplierName		VARCHAR2(20)	NOT NULL,
Description			VARCHAR2(50)	NOT NULL,
SupplierEmail		VARCHAR2(28)	CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(SupplierEmail,'^[a-zA-Z]\w+@(\S+)$')),
SupplierPhoneNo		VARCHAR2(15)	CHECK (REGEXP_LIKE(SupplierPhoneNo,'^0[0-9]{2}-[0-9]{7}$')),
SupplierAddress 		VARCHAR2(30)	NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY(SupplierID)
);

--200
CREATE TABLE Product(
ProductID			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
ProductName			VARCHAR2(25)	NOT NULL,
ProductPrice		NUMBER(5,2)		NOT NULL,
Stock				NUMBER(3)		DEFAULT 50,
ProductWeight		NUMBER(4,2)		NOT NULL,
Category			VARCHAR2(67)	NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY(ProductID)
);

--200
CREATE TABLE Review(
ReviewID		VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
CustomerRating	NUMBER(1)		DEFAULT 1,
CustomerComment	VARCHAR2(90)	NOT NULL, 
DateCreated		DATE			NOT NULL,
CustomerID 	 	VARCHAR2(10) 	NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY(ReviewID),
FOREIGN KEY(CustomerID) REFERENCES Customer(CustomerID)
);

--200
CREATE TABLE Orders(
OrderID 			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
OrderDate			DATE			NOT NULL,
OrderStatus 		VARCHAR2(15),
TotalWeight			NUMBER(5,2),
TotalPrice			NUMBER(9,2),
DiscountAmount		NUMBER(4,2) 	DEFAULT 0,
CustomerID 	 		VARCHAR2(10) 	NOT NULL,
DiscountID 			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
PaymentID			VARCHAR2(10),
DeliveryID			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
RefundID			VARCHAR2(10),
PRIMARY KEY(OrderID),
FOREIGN KEY(CustomerID) REFERENCES Customer(CustomerID),
FOREIGN KEY(DiscountID) REFERENCES Discount(DiscountID),
FOREIGN KEY(PaymentID) REFERENCES Payment(PaymentID),
FOREIGN KEY(DeliveryID) REFERENCES Delivery(DeliveryID),
FOREIGN KEY(RefundID) REFERENCES Refund(RefundID)
);


--600
CREATE TABLE OrderDetail(
OrderID 			VARCHAR2(20)	NOT NULL,
ProductID			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
ProductQuantity		NUMBER(2)		DEFAULT 1,
SubTotal			NUMBER(7,2),
ReviewID			VARCHAR2(10),
PRIMARY KEY(OrderID,ProductID),
FOREIGN KEY(OrderID) REFERENCES Orders(OrderID),
FOREIGN KEY(ProductID) REFERENCES Product(ProductID),
FOREIGN KEY(ReviewID) REFERENCES Review(ReviewID)
);

--600
CREATE TABLE PurchaseOrder(
PurchaseOrderID		VARCHAR2(15)	NOT NULL,
ProductID			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
SupplierID 			VARCHAR2(10)	NOT NULL,
Quantity			NUMBER(4)		DEFAULT 1,
SupplierOrderDate		DATE			NOT NULL,
UnitPrice			NUMBER(6,2)		NOT NULL,
TotalPrice			NUMBER(9,2),
PRIMARY KEY(SupplierID,ProductID,PurchaseOrderID),
FOREIGN KEY(SupplierID) REFERENCES Supplier(SupplierID),
FOREIGN KEY(ProductID) REFERENCES Product(ProductID)
);


--INDEX
CREATE INDEX idx_customer
ON Customer (CustomerName);

CREATE INDEX idx_delivery
ON Delivery (DepartureDate, ArrivedDate);

CREATE INDEX idx_payment
ON Payment (PaymentDate);

CREATE INDEX idx_refund
ON Refund (RefundDate);

CREATE INDEX idx_staff
ON Staff (StaffName);

CREATE INDEX idx_discount
ON Discount (DiscountName);

CREATE INDEX idx_supplier
ON Supplier (SupplierName);

CREATE INDEX idx_product
ON Product (ProductName, ProductPrice, Stock, ProductWeight);

CREATE INDEX idx_review
ON Review (CustomerRating, DateCreated);

CREATE INDEX idx_orders
ON Orders (OrderDate, TotalWeight, TotalPrice, DiscountAmount);

CREATE INDEX idx_orderdetail
ON OrderDetail (ProductQuantity, SubTotal);

CREATE INDEX idx_purchaseorder
ON PurchaseOrder(Quantity, SupplierOrderDate, UnitPrice, TotalPrice);

From Customer;

select count(*) as noOfStaff
From Staff;

From Orders;

From orderdetail;

From Delivery;

From Payment;

From Review;

From Refund;

From Product;

From PurchaseOrder;

From Supplier;

From Discount;
